                      <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="1822">
                       <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="1823">
                        Arizona Oasis RV Resort, formerly known as Colorado River Oasis RV Resort is an exciting retreat where people of all ages can come to get away from it all and spend some time on the river. Our affordable trailers are clean and cozy for your long or short term needs. Trailers are equipped with a nice shower, kitchen, and come fully furnished with a TV and queen size bed. Some units offer a pull out couch or a dinette that makes into a bed.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="1824">
                        RV trailer rentals have the convenience of being equipped with basic items to make your stay more enjoyable which include: a coffee pot (bring your own filters and coffee), toaster, setting of 4 dishes, silverware, and glasses. Pots &amp; pans, pot holders &amp; kitchen towels, kitchen utensils &amp; knives, set of 2 bath towels (laundry available in Clubhouse), bedding for one bed. Bring additional bedding if you plan on using a pull out bed in your unit. You will receive one code that can be used to connect to our WiFi. Additional codes are available for purchase at the office. The rental includes cable. A 5 lane boat launch will get your in and out of the river fast. 2 beach areas for landing your tubes, kayaks, boats and more make it convenient for you to get on land. Clubhouse amenities like swimming pool (and kiddy pool!) hot tub, showers and more add to your getaway experience.
                       </div>

                       <div class="listing__seo-reviews" data-reactid="1826">
                        <li data-reactid="1827"><p data-reactid="1828">My Fiance and I, enjoyed the Arizona Oasis. The trailer we stayed in wasn't huge but was nice and cozy. It has a nice little fridge so we could store food and cook it later. The smoke alarm is a bit sensitive so if you going to be cooking open all the windows. The bed is nice. My man is tall and the bed is short, so his feet hung off the bed. So, that's a thing for the tall people. The staff was really nice and helped us out very quickly when we were having a problem with the toilet drain. I don't think the pipes were flushed out correctly or at all. So, when we first arrived there was a slight smell to the RV. All was well though the staff was on top of it, when we told them. The resort is quiet. People staying there are friendly. The clubhouse has a pool table that anyone can use. You can watch DVDs on the big screen TV. There is hammocks hung down by the river. Plus, they let you use the firewood down by the burn pit. The stars are incredibly especially when your sitting in the hot tub. The pool and hot tub have clean water and are not too chlorinated. All together we had a lovely stay. Very peaceful vacation. We would come back again. </p><span data-reactid="1829">Rachel</span><span data-reactid="1830">2017-03-22T00:00:00Z</span></li>
